[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing session against the Apache Commons Compress “Expander” example [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered a critical security alert for file path traversal. During unpacking, a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrafted archive entry containing “..” segments caused the sanitizer [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FilePathTraversal.check` to throw `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`, indicating that [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction would escape the intended output directory.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer provided input to `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` that resulted in a computed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile path `[0m[35m/tmp/[0m[39m…[0m[35m/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`. When the code attempted to write[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor create this path, Jazzer’s `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer detected an escape [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m“..”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m outside the designated extraction folder and raised a security exception.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a classic file path traversal vulnerability: archive entries can [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreference parent directories and thereby overwrite or create files outside of the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended extraction root.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.check` → `checkPath` → [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`pathFirstArgHook`.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace bubbles up through multiple overloads of [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m460[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness method `ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` is merely the entry [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoint; it feeds arbitrary bytes to `Expander`, but is not the root cause.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander.expand` and its [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternal methods that build target file paths from archive entry names.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnormalization, sanitization[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m around handling of “..” segments in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile names.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Integration with the `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer hooks to understand which [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs bypass or trigger the check.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any auxiliary utilities in Commons Compress that resolve or sanitize file paths[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprior to creating `File` or `Path` objects.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA review of these areas will give a holistic understanding of how path [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization and security checks interact, and where untrusted entry names may [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mslip through.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:                if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnullTarget[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, NullOutputStream.INSTANCE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:                    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOutputStream outputStream = [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mFiles.newOutputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtargetPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;35mwriter.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnextEntry, outputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The default implementation of ArchiveEntry.resolveIn:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a. Resolves the raw entry name against the parent path and normalizes that [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitial Path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`outputFile`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b. Checks for directory traversal by ensuring [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     c. **Then** returns `[0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` **without** [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many normalization step, re-introducing “..” segments when the decoded name contains[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - As a result, downstream callers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., Expander.expand[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m receive an [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munnormalized Path containing “..” and attempt to write to it. Jazzer’s [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFilePathTraversal sanitizer then flags this as escaping the intended directory.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy Overview[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Always return a **fully normalized** Path from `resolveIn`, **after** [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mURL-decoding the entry name.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Combine the decode, resolve, normalize, and safety-check into a single, atomic[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperation.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the two-step resolve→normalize→check→decode→resolve pattern, replacing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit with:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfallback to `name` on [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `resolved = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. If `![0m[1;35mresolved.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, throw `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m..."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Return `resolved`[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocate the `default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m78[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m89[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace its body with the following logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpseudocode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Attempt URL decoding once[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String decodedName;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m[1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          decodedName = name;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Resolve and normalize in one go[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Security check[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, parentPath, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecodedName, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Return the safe, normalized Path[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      return outputFile;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Remove the original two-call approach [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfirst resolving raw, then resolving [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecoded[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to avoid any “..” slipping through after the check.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. No changes are needed in Expander; it will continue to call [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mentry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and operate on the normalized, safe Path.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Security**: By decoding and normalizing **before** the directory-escape [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck, we guarantee that no “..” segments remain in the returned Path. This [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevents downstream code from ever seeing a Path that escapes the target directory.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Behavior Preservation**:  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Existing logic for URL decoding is maintained [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfallback on exception[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Exception message is preserved in spirit, only reflecting the decoded name [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of the raw name.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No change to how Expander writes or extracts; only the Path returned is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafer.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Minimal Impact**:  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Only affects the `resolveIn` helper method.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • No modifications to fuzzing harness, external libraries, tests, or other [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutilities.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • All existing test suites and usage of `resolveIn` will use the new logic [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseamlessly.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side-Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Percent-encoded entry names will continue to be decoded exactly once.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If users rely on the old behavior of a double-resolution, their tests may [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnotice slightly different exception messages [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnow showing decoded name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Adjust [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest assertions if they rely on the exact message.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No impact on other archive formats, since the change is generic to all [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ArchiveEntry` implementations.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar logic is already applied in other secure unzip examples: decode → [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolve → normalize → check → use.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This pattern matches OWASP recommendations for Zip Slip prevention.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         The fuzzer run on Apache Commons Compress triggered a Jazzer security issue for     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         file path traversal when unpacking archive entries with malicious names [1m([0me.g.,      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         containing “..[35m/[0m”[1m)[0m. The user’s patch changed the `resolveIn` method in               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ArchiveEntry.java` to URL-decode the entry name before resolving and               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         normalization, and to centralize the traversal check using a single `decodedName`   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         variable. After applying the patch, the build fails with a Java compilation error:  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “variable decodedName might already have been assigned”.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - A Jazzer run on the `ExpanderFuzzer` produced a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exception citing “File path traversal” on a path like                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[35m/tmp/[0m[95mexpander-[0m…[35m/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The stack trace shows the failure in the Jazzer sanitizer                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`, invoked from `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` in the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Commons Compress example code.                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - This indicates that when expanding archive entries, a malicious entry name with   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “..[35m/[0m” components was not properly neutralized, allowing the resolved output path to [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         escape the intended parent directory.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The user edited `[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath parentPath[1m)[0m` in                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - They introduced a local `decodedName` string, set by `[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1m([0mname,     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         US_ASCII[1m)[0m`. On decode errors they fall back to the original `name`.                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - They replaced the two-step resolve-and-decode logic with a single normalized      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `outputFile = [1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mdecodedName[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - A single traversal check [1m([0m`![1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1m([0mparentPath[1m)[0m`[1m)[0m throws an         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `IOException` if the entry escapes.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The method now returns the validated `outputFile`.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Resulting Build Log                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - When recompiling via Maven, the compiler reports:                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           `[35m/src/commons-compress/src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/[0m[95mArchiv[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95meEntry.java[0m:[1m[[0m[1;36m84[0m,[1;36m13[0m[1m][0m variable decodedName might already have been assigned`          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - This indicates that the patch’s control flow allows a code path in which          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `decodedName` could be assigned twice, leading to a definite assignment conflict.   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Areas for Further Investigation                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The implementation of `ArchiveEntry.resolveIn`: verify all control-flow paths for [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `decodedName` assignment and ensure only a single, unambiguous declaration and      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         assignment.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Usage sites of `resolveIn` in `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` to understand how entry      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         names are passed and whether additional normalization is needed.                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The interplay between Commons Compress’s path-handling logic and the Jazzer       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer hooks: confirm that all file-opening and              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         directory-creation calls go through the sanitization check.                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Potential related code in other archive formats [1m([0me.g., tar, zip[1m)[0m where similar    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path resolution occurs.                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Rework `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to decode the entry name before[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many resolution or normalization, perform a single reserve-and-normalize pass, then [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menforce the directory‐escape check on the decoded path. This both neutralizes [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mencoded “..[0m[35m/[0m[39m” attacks and simplifies control flow to eliminate the compile‐time [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“definite assignment” error.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. In `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreplace the existing default implementation of `resolveIn` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m78[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m89[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfollowing logic:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Read the raw name:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String name = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Initialize a mutable `decodedName` to the raw `name`:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      String decodedName = name;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Attempt URL‐decode, silently falling back on any exception:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m[1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m invalid or unsupported encoding: use raw name[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Resolve and normalize once, using the decoded name:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Enforce that the normalized `outputFile` remains under `parentPath`. If not, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrow `IOException` with the decoded name in the message:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m,[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              parentPath, decodedName, outputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f. Return the safe, normalized `outputFile`:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      return outputFile;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. This eliminates the two‐step resolve‐check‐decode logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand its missing second [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, guarantees coverage of encoded traversal sequences, and prevents the Java [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompiler’s “variable might already have been assigned” error by ensuring [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`decodedName` is always initialized [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto `name`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before the `try`.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. No other modifications to harness code, external dependencies, or tests are [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequired. The change preserves existing functionality for well‐formed entry names, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcentralizes URL‐decoding up front, and applies a single, consistent safety check [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magainst directory escapes. [0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
